            <script class="element-script" type="text/javascript">
             function setupElement358092108639912713() {
 	var requireFunc = window.platformElementRequire || window.require;
 
 	// Relies on a global require, specific to platform elements
 	requireFunc([
 		'w-global',
 		'underscore',
 		'jquery',
 		'backbone',
 		'util/platform/elements/PlatformElement',
 		'util/platform/elements/PlatformElementSettings'
 	], function(
 		_W,
 		_,
 		$,
 		Backbone,
 		PlatformElement,
 		PlatformElementSettings
 	) {
 		var dependencies = null || [];
 		var platform_element_id = "740308791667012911-1.1.6";
 
 		if (typeof _W.loadedPlatformDependencies === 'undefined') {
 			_W.loadedPlatformDependencies = [];
 		}
 
 		if (typeof _W.platformElements === 'undefined') {
 			_W.platformElements = [];
 		}
 
 		if (typeof _W.platformElements[platform_element_id] === 'undefined') {
 			_W.platformElements[platform_element_id] = {};
 			_W.platformElements[platform_element_id].deferredObject = new $.Deferred();
 			_W.platformElements[platform_element_id].deferredPromise = _W.platformElements[platform_element_id].deferredObject.promise();
 		}
 
 		if(_.intersection(_W.loadedPlatformDependencies, dependencies).length !== dependencies.length){
 			_.reduce(dependencies, function(promise, nextScript){
 				_W.loadedPlatformDependencies.push(nextScript);
 				return promise.then(function(){
 					return $.getScript(nextScript);
 				});
 			}, $().promise()).then(function(){
 				_W.platformElements[platform_element_id].deferredObject.resolve();
 			});
 		}
 
 		if (dependencies.length === 0){
 			_W.platformElements[platform_element_id].deferredObject.resolve();
 		}
 
 		_W.platformElements[platform_element_id].deferredPromise.done(function(){
 			var _ElementDefinition = (function() {
 	var booTestimonialSlider = PlatformElement.extend({
 		initialize: function() {
 			this._inner				= this.$(".booTestimonialInner");
 			this._content			= this.$(".booTestimonialContentWrap");
 			this._total				= this.settings.get("total");
 			this._bullet			= this.$(".booTestimonialControls li");
 			this._autoSlide			= this.settings.get("autoSlide");
 			this._stopOnHover		= this.settings.get("stopOnHover");
 			this._size				= 0;
 			this._startScroll		= 0;
 			this._innerMargin		= 0;
 			this._startX			= 0;
 			this._startY			= 0;
 			this._offsetX			= 0;
 			this._offsetY			= 0;
 			this._distancePercent	= 0;
 			this._clicked			= false;
 			this._isTouchDevice		= false;
 			this._isScrolling		= false;
 			this._bullet.first().addClass("active");
 			this.setupTestimonialSlider();
         },
 		events: {
 			"click .booTestimonialControls li": "clickScroll",
 			"mousedown .booTestimonialControls li": "clickScroll",
 			"touchstart .booTestimonialControls li": "clickScroll",
 			"mousedown .booTestimonialSlider": "touchStart",
 			"touchstart .booTestimonialSlider": "touchStart",
 			"mousemove .booTestimonialSlider": "touchMove",
 			"touchmove .booTestimonialSlider": "touchMove",
 			"mouseup .booTestimonialSlider": "touchEnd",
 			"touchend .booTestimonialSlider": "touchEnd"
 		},
 
 		clickScroll: function(e){
 			var active	= $(e.currentTarget);
 			var slide	= active.data("slide");
 			var _this	= this;
 
 			//Slide content
 			if(typeof _this._inner!=='undefined'){
 				_this._inner.css({
 					"margin-left": -1*slide*100+"%"
 				});
 				var _height		= this.$(".booTestimonialSlideContent").eq(slide).find(".booTestimonial").outerHeight();
 				this.$(".booTestimonialSlideContent").animate({
 					height: _height+25
 				})
 			}
 			// Set new active bullets
 			active.siblings().removeClass('active');
             active.addClass('active');
 			if(_this._autoSlide>0){
 				if(_this._startScroll){
 					clearInterval(_this._startScroll);
 				}
 				_this._startScroll	= setInterval(function(){
 					_this.next();
 				},  _this._autoSlide*1000);
 				if(_this._stopOnHover){
 					//Hover to stop
 					_this.$(".booTestimonialSlider").hover(function(){
 						if(_this._startScroll){
 							clearInterval(_this._startScroll);
 							console.log("stop "+_this._startScroll);
 						}
 					}, function(){
 						//Hold on 50% auto start time to re-sliding
 						setTimeout(function(){
 							if(_this._startScroll){
 								clearInterval(_this._startScroll);
 							}
 							_this._startScroll	= setInterval(function(){
 								_this.next();
 							},  _this._autoSlide*1000);
 						}, Math.round(_this._autoSlide/2)*1000);
 					});
 				}
 			}
 		},
 		
 		touchStart: function(e){
 			var ev				= this._isTouchDevice?e.originalEvent.touches[0]:e;
 			this._startX		= ev.clientX;
 			this._startY		= ev.clientY;
 			this._clicked		= true;
 			if(typeof this._inner!=='undefined'){
 				this._innerMargin	= this._inner.css("margin-left");
 			}
 			this._offsetX		= this.$(".booTestimonialSlider").offset().left;
 			this._offsetY		= this.$(".booTestimonialSlider").offset().top;
 			this._size			= this.$(".booTestimonialSlider").width();
 			if(this._startScroll){
 				clearInterval(this._startScroll);
 			}
 		},
 
 		touchMove: function(e){
 			if(this._isScrolling){
 				return;
 			}
 			if(!this._clicked){
 				return;
 			}
 			var ev			= this._isTouchDevice?e.originalEvent.touches[0]:e;
 			//Detect scrolling
 			if(Math.abs(ev.clientY - this._startY)>8 && Math.abs(ev.clientX - this._startX)<20){
 				this._isScrolling	= true;
 			}else{
 				e.preventDefault();
 			}
 			//Moved out of testimonials wrap
 			if(ev.clientX <= (this._offsetX + this._size*0.05) || ev.clientX >= (this._offsetX + this._size*0.95)){
 				this.touchEnd();
 				return;
 			}
 			
 			var distance			= ev.clientX - this._startX;
 			this._distancePercent	= (distance/this._size)*100;
 			distance				= parseFloat(distance)+parseFloat(this._innerMargin);
 			if(typeof this._inner!=='undefined'){
 				this._inner.addClass("dragging").css({
 					"margin-left": distance
 				});
 			}
 		},
 
 		touchEnd: function(e){
